697struct BuiltinOptionsUnion {
698 BuiltinOptions type;
699 void *value;
700
701 BuiltinOptionsUnion() : type(BuiltinOptions_NONE), value(nullptr) {}
702 BuiltinOptionsUnion(BuiltinOptionsUnion&& u) FLATBUFFERS_NOEXCEPT :
703 type(BuiltinOptions_NONE), value(nullptr)
704 { std::swap(type, u.type); std::swap(value, u.value); }
705 BuiltinOptionsUnion(const BuiltinOptionsUnion &) FLATBUFFERS_NOEXCEPT;
706 BuiltinOptionsUnion &operator=(const BuiltinOptionsUnion &u) FLATBUFFERS_NOEXCEPT
707 { BuiltinOptionsUnion t(u); std::swap(type, t.type); std::swap(value, t.value); return *this; }
708 BuiltinOptionsUnion &operator=(BuiltinOptionsUnion &&u) FLATBUFFERS_NOEXCEPT
709 { std::swap(type, u.type); std::swap(value, u.value); return *this; }
710 ~BuiltinOptionsUnion() { Reset(); }

712 void Reset();

714#ifndef FLATBUFFERS_CPP98_STL
715 template <typename T>
716 void Set(T&& val) {
717 Reset();
718 type = BuiltinOptionsTraits<typename T::TableType>::enum_value;
719 if (type != BuiltinOptions_NONE) {
720 value = new T(std::forward<T>(val));
721 }
722 }
723#endif // FLATBUFFERS_CPP98_STL

1205struct QuantizationParametersT : public flatbuffers::NativeTable {
1206 typedef QuantizationParameters TableType;
1207 std::vector<float> min;
1208 std::vector<float> max;
1209 std::vector<float> scale;
1210 std::vector<int64_t> zero_point;
1211 QuantizationParametersT() {
1212 }
1213};
1214
1215struct QuantizationParameters FLATBUFFERS_FINAL_CLASS : private flatbuffers::Table {
1216 typedef QuantizationParametersT NativeTableType;
1217 enum {
1218 VT_MIN = 4,
1219 VT_MAX = 6,
1220 VT_SCALE = 8,
1221 VT_ZERO_POINT = 10
1222 };
1223 const flatbuffers::Vector<float> *min() const {
1224 return GetPointer<const flatbuffers::Vector<float> *>(VT_MIN);
1225 }
1226 const flatbuffers::Vector<float> *max() const {
1227 return GetPointer<const flatbuffers::Vector<float> *>(VT_MAX);
1228 }
1229 const flatbuffers::Vector<float> *scale() const {
1230 return GetPointer<const flatbuffers::Vector<float> *>(VT_SCALE);
1231 }
1232 const flatbuffers::Vector<int64_t> *zero_point() const {
1233 return GetPointer<const flatbuffers::Vector<int64_t> *>(VT_ZERO_POINT);
1234 }
1235 bool Verify(flatbuffers::Verifier &verifier) const {
1236 return VerifyTableStart(verifier) &&
1237 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_MIN) &&
1238 verifier.Verify(min()) &&
1239 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_MAX) &&
1240 verifier.Verify(max()) &&
1241 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_SCALE) &&
1242 verifier.Verify(scale()) &&
1243 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_ZERO_POINT) &&
1244 verifier.Verify(zero_point()) &&
1245 verifier.EndTable();
1246 }
1247 QuantizationParametersT *UnPack(const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *_resolver = nullptr) const;
1248 void UnPackTo(QuantizationParametersT *_o, const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *_resolver = nullptr) const;
1249 static flatbuffers::Offset<QuantizationParameters> Pack(flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb, const QuantizationParametersT* _o, const flatbuffers::rehasher_function_t *_rehasher = nullptr);
1250};
1251
1252struct QuantizationParametersBuilder {
1253 flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &fbb_;
1254 flatbuffers::uoffset_t start_;
1255 void add_min(flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<float>> min) {
1256 fbb_.AddOffset(QuantizationParameters::VT_MIN, min);
1257 }
1258 void add_max(flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<float>> max) {
1259 fbb_.AddOffset(QuantizationParameters::VT_MAX, max);
1260 }
1261 void add_scale(flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<float>> scale) {
1262 fbb_.AddOffset(QuantizationParameters::VT_SCALE, scale);
1263 }
1264 void add_zero_point(flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<int64_t>> zero_point) {
1265 fbb_.AddOffset(QuantizationParameters::VT_ZERO_POINT, zero_point);
1266 }
1267 explicit QuantizationParametersBuilder(flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb)
1268 : fbb_(_fbb) {
1269 start_ = fbb_.StartTable();
1270 }
1271 QuantizationParametersBuilder &operator=(const QuantizationParametersBuilder &);
1272 flatbuffers::Offset<QuantizationParameters> Finish() {
1273 const auto end = fbb_.EndTable(start_);
1274 auto o = flatbuffers::Offset<QuantizationParameters>(end);
1275 return o;
1276 }
1277};
1278
1279inline flatbuffers::Offset<QuantizationParameters> CreateQuantizationParameters(
1280 flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb,
1281 flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<float>> min = 0,
1282 flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<float>> max = 0,
1283 flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<float>> scale = 0,
1284 flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<int64_t>> zero_point = 0) {
1285 QuantizationParametersBuilder builder_(_fbb);
1286 builder_.add_zero_point(zero_point);
1287 builder_.add_scale(scale);
1288 builder_.add_max(max);
1289 builder_.add_min(min);
1290 return builder_.Finish();
1291}
1292
1293inline flatbuffers::Offset<QuantizationParameters> CreateQuantizationParametersDirect(
1294 flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb,
1295 const std::vector<float> *min = nullptr,
1296 const std::vector<float> *max = nullptr,
1297 const std::vector<float> *scale = nullptr,
1298 const std::vector<int64_t> *zero_point = nullptr) {
1299 return tflite::CreateQuantizationParameters(
1300 _fbb,
1301 min ? _fbb.CreateVector<float>(*min) : 0,
1302 max ? _fbb.CreateVector<float>(*max) : 0,
1303 scale ? _fbb.CreateVector<float>(*scale) : 0,
1304 zero_point ? _fbb.CreateVector<int64_t>(*zero_point) : 0);
1305}
1306
1307flatbuffers::Offset<QuantizationParameters> CreateQuantizationParameters(flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb, const QuantizationParametersT *_o, const flatbuffers::rehasher_function_t *_rehasher = nullptr);
1308
1309struct TensorT : public flatbuffers::NativeTable {
1310 typedef Tensor TableType;
1311 std::vector<int32_t> shape;
1312 TensorType type;
1313 uint32_t buffer;
1314 std::string name;
1315 std::unique_ptr<QuantizationParametersT> quantization;
1316 TensorT()
1317 : type(TensorType_FLOAT32),
1318 buffer(0) {
1319 }
1320};
1321
1322struct Tensor FLATBUFFERS_FINAL_CLASS : private flatbuffers::Table {
1323 typedef TensorT NativeTableType;
1324 enum {
1325 VT_SHAPE = 4,
1326 VT_TYPE = 6,
1327 VT_BUFFER = 8,
1328 VT_NAME = 10,
1329 VT_QUANTIZATION = 12
1330 };
1331 const flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t> *shape() const {
1332 return GetPointer<const flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t> *>(VT_SHAPE);
1333 }
1334 TensorType type() const {
1335 return static_cast<TensorType>(GetField<int8_t>(VT_TYPE, 0));
1336 }
1337 uint32_t buffer() const {
1338 return GetField<uint32_t>(VT_BUFFER, 0);
1339 }
1340 const flatbuffers::String *name() const {
1341 return GetPointer<const flatbuffers::String *>(VT_NAME);
1342 }
1343 const QuantizationParameters *quantization() const {
1344 return GetPointer<const QuantizationParameters *>(VT_QUANTIZATION);
1345 }
1346 bool Verify(flatbuffers::Verifier &verifier) const {
1347 return VerifyTableStart(verifier) &&
1348 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_SHAPE) &&
1349 verifier.Verify(shape()) &&
1350 VerifyField<int8_t>(verifier, VT_TYPE) &&
1351 VerifyField<uint32_t>(verifier, VT_BUFFER) &&
1352 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_NAME) &&
1353 verifier.Verify(name()) &&
1354 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_QUANTIZATION) &&
1355 verifier.VerifyTable(quantization()) &&
1356 verifier.EndTable();
1357 }
1358 TensorT *UnPack(const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *_resolver = nullptr) const;
1359 void UnPackTo(TensorT *_o, const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *_resolver = nullptr) const;
1360 static flatbuffers::Offset<Tensor> Pack(flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb, const TensorT* _o, const flatbuffers::rehasher_function_t *_rehasher = nullptr);
1361};
1362
1363struct TensorBuilder {
1364 flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &fbb_;
1365 flatbuffers::uoffset_t start_;
1366 void add_shape(flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t>> shape) {
1367 fbb_.AddOffset(Tensor::VT_SHAPE, shape);
1368 }
1369 void add_type(TensorType type) {
1370 fbb_.AddElement<int8_t>(Tensor::VT_TYPE, static_cast<int8_t>(type), 0);
1371 }
1372 void add_buffer(uint32_t buffer) {
1373 fbb_.AddElement<uint32_t>(Tensor::VT_BUFFER, buffer, 0);
1374 }
1375 void add_name(flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::String> name) {
1376 fbb_.AddOffset(Tensor::VT_NAME, name);
1377 }
1378 void add_quantization(flatbuffers::Offset<QuantizationParameters> quantization) {
1379 fbb_.AddOffset(Tensor::VT_QUANTIZATION, quantization);
1380 }
1381 explicit TensorBuilder(flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb)
1382 : fbb_(_fbb) {
1383 start_ = fbb_.StartTable();
1384 }
1385 TensorBuilder &operator=(const TensorBuilder &);
1386 flatbuffers::Offset<Tensor> Finish() {
1387 const auto end = fbb_.EndTable(start_);
1388 auto o = flatbuffers::Offset<Tensor>(end);
1389 return o;
1390 }
1391};
1392
1393inline flatbuffers::Offset<Tensor> CreateTensor(
1394 flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb,
1395 flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t>> shape = 0,
1396 TensorType type = TensorType_FLOAT32,
1397 uint32_t buffer = 0,
1398 flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::String> name = 0,
1399 flatbuffers::Offset<QuantizationParameters> quantization = 0) {
1400 TensorBuilder builder_(_fbb);
1401 builder_.add_quantization(quantization);
1402 builder_.add_name(name);
1403 builder_.add_buffer(buffer);
1404 builder_.add_shape(shape);
1405 builder_.add_type(type);
1406 return builder_.Finish();
1407}
1408
1409inline flatbuffers::Offset<Tensor> CreateTensorDirect(
1410 flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb,
1411 const std::vector<int32_t> *shape = nullptr,
1412 TensorType type = TensorType_FLOAT32,
1413 uint32_t buffer = 0,
1414 const char *name = nullptr,
1415 flatbuffers::Offset<QuantizationParameters> quantization = 0) {
1416 return tflite::CreateTensor(
1417 _fbb,
1418 shape ? _fbb.CreateVector<int32_t>(*shape) : 0,
1419 type,
1420 buffer,
1421 name ? _fbb.CreateString(name) : 0,
1422 quantization);
1423}

1425flatbuffers::Offset<Tensor> CreateTensor(flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb, const TensorT *_o, const flatbuffers::rehasher_function_t *_rehasher = nullptr);

1427struct Conv2DOptionsT : public flatbuffers::NativeTable {
1428 typedef Conv2DOptions TableType;
1429 Padding padding;
1430 int32_t stride_w;
1431 int32_t stride_h;
1432 ActivationFunctionType fused_activation_function;
1433 Conv2DOptionsT()
1434 : padding(Padding_SAME),
1435 stride_w(0),
1436 stride_h(0),
1437 fused_activation_function(ActivationFunctionType_NONE) {
1438 }
1439};

1441struct Conv2DOptions FLATBUFFERS_FINAL_CLASS : private flatbuffers::Table {
1442 typedef Conv2DOptionsT NativeTableType;
1443 enum {
1444 VT_PADDING = 4,
1445 VT_STRIDE_W = 6,
1446 VT_STRIDE_H = 8,
1447 VT_FUSED_ACTIVATION_FUNCTION = 10
1448 };
1449 Padding padding() const {
1450 return static_cast<Padding>(GetField<int8_t>(VT_PADDING, 0));
1451 }
1452 int32_t stride_w() const {
1453 return GetField<int32_t>(VT_STRIDE_W, 0);
1454 }
1455 int32_t stride_h() const {
1456 return GetField<int32_t>(VT_STRIDE_H, 0);
1457 }
1458 ActivationFunctionType fused_activation_function() const {
1459 return static_cast<ActivationFunctionType>(GetField<int8_t>(VT_FUSED_ACTIVATION_FUNCTION, 0));
1460 }
1461 bool Verify(flatbuffers::Verifier &verifier) const {
1462 return VerifyTableStart(verifier) &&
1463 VerifyField<int8_t>(verifier, VT_PADDING) &&
1464 VerifyField<int32_t>(verifier, VT_STRIDE_W) &&
1465 VerifyField<int32_t>(verifier, VT_STRIDE_H) &&
1466 VerifyField<int8_t>(verifier, VT_FUSED_ACTIVATION_FUNCTION) &&
1467 verifier.EndTable();
1468 }
1469 Conv2DOptionsT *UnPack(const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *_resolver = nullptr) const;
1470 void UnPackTo(Conv2DOptionsT *_o, const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *_resolver = nullptr) const;
1471 static flatbuffers::Offset<Conv2DOptions> Pack(flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb, const Conv2DOptionsT* _o, const flatbuffers::rehasher_function_t *_rehasher = nullptr);
1472};

1484 fbb_.AddElement<int32_t>(Conv2DOptions::VT_STRIDE_H, stride_h, 0);

1487 fbb_.AddElement<int8_t>(Conv2DOptions::VT_FUSED_ACTIVATION_FUNCTION, static_cast<int8_t>(fused_activation_function), 0);

1501inline flatbuffers::Offset<Conv2DOptions> CreateConv2DOptions(
1502 flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb,
1503 Padding padding = Padding_SAME,
1504 int32_t stride_w = 0,
1505 int32_t stride_h = 0,
1506 ActivationFunctionType fused_activation_function = ActivationFunctionType_NONE) {
1507 Conv2DOptionsBuilder builder_(_fbb);
1508 builder_.add_stride_h(stride_h);
1509 builder_.add_stride_w(stride_w);
1510 builder_.add_fused_activation_function(fused_activation_function);
1511 builder_.add_padding(padding);
1512 return builder_.Finish();
1513}

1733struct ConcatEmbeddingsOptionsT : public flatbuffers::NativeTable {
1734 typedef ConcatEmbeddingsOptions TableType;
1735 int32_t num_channels;
1736 std::vector<int32_t> num_columns_per_channel;
1737 std::vector<int32_t> embedding_dim_per_channel;
1738 ConcatEmbeddingsOptionsT()
1739 : num_channels(0) {
1740 }
1741};
1742
1743struct ConcatEmbeddingsOptions FLATBUFFERS_FINAL_CLASS : private flatbuffers::Table {
1744 typedef ConcatEmbeddingsOptionsT NativeTableType;
1745 enum {
1746 VT_NUM_CHANNELS = 4,
1747 VT_NUM_COLUMNS_PER_CHANNEL = 6,
1748 VT_EMBEDDING_DIM_PER_CHANNEL = 8
1749 };
1750 int32_t num_channels() const {
1751 return GetField<int32_t>(VT_NUM_CHANNELS, 0);
1752 }
1753 const flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t> *num_columns_per_channel() const {
1754 return GetPointer<const flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t> *>(VT_NUM_COLUMNS_PER_CHANNEL);
1755 }
1756 const flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t> *embedding_dim_per_channel() const {
1757 return GetPointer<const flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t> *>(VT_EMBEDDING_DIM_PER_CHANNEL);
1758 }
1759 bool Verify(flatbuffers::Verifier &verifier) const {
1760 return VerifyTableStart(verifier) &&
1761 VerifyField<int32_t>(verifier, VT_NUM_CHANNELS) &&
1762 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_NUM_COLUMNS_PER_CHANNEL) &&
1763 verifier.Verify(num_columns_per_channel()) &&
1764 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_EMBEDDING_DIM_PER_CHANNEL) &&
1765 verifier.Verify(embedding_dim_per_channel()) &&
1766 verifier.EndTable();
1767 }
1768 ConcatEmbeddingsOptionsT *UnPack(const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *_resolver = nullptr) const;
1769 void UnPackTo(ConcatEmbeddingsOptionsT *_o, const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *_resolver = nullptr) const;
1770 static flatbuffers::Offset<ConcatEmbeddingsOptions> Pack(flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb, const ConcatEmbeddingsOptionsT* _o, const flatbuffers::rehasher_function_t *_rehasher = nullptr);
1771};

1780 fbb_.AddOffset(ConcatEmbeddingsOptions::VT_NUM_COLUMNS_PER_CHANNEL, num_columns_per_channel);
1781 }
1782 void add_embedding_dim_per_channel(flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t>> embedding_dim_per_channel) {

1797inline flatbuffers::Offset<ConcatEmbeddingsOptions> CreateConcatEmbeddingsOptions(
1798 flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb,
1799 int32_t num_channels = 0,
1800 flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t>> num_columns_per_channel = 0,
1801 flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t>> embedding_dim_per_channel = 0) {
1802 ConcatEmbeddingsOptionsBuilder builder_(_fbb);
1803 builder_.add_embedding_dim_per_channel(embedding_dim_per_channel);
1804 builder_.add_num_columns_per_channel(num_columns_per_channel);
1805 builder_.add_num_channels(num_channels);
1806 return builder_.Finish();
1807}

1809inline flatbuffers::Offset<ConcatEmbeddingsOptions> CreateConcatEmbeddingsOptionsDirect(
1810 flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb,
1811 int32_t num_channels = 0,
1812 const std::vector<int32_t> *num_columns_per_channel = nullptr,
1813 const std::vector<int32_t> *embedding_dim_per_channel = nullptr) {
1814 return tflite::CreateConcatEmbeddingsOptions(
1815 _fbb,
1816 num_channels,
1817 num_columns_per_channel ? _fbb.CreateVector<int32_t>(*num_columns_per_channel) : 0,
1818 embedding_dim_per_channel ? _fbb.CreateVector<int32_t>(*embedding_dim_per_channel) : 0);
1819}

2485 VT_BETA = 10

2488 return GetField<int32_t>(VT_RADIUS, 0);
2489 }
2490 float bias() const {
2491 return GetField<float>(VT_BIAS, 0.0f);
2492 }
2493 float alpha() const {
2494 return GetField<float>(VT_ALPHA, 0.0f);
2495 }

2497 return GetField<float>(VT_BETA, 0.0f);
2498 }

2500 return VerifyTableStart(verifier) &&
2501 VerifyField<int32_t>(verifier, VT_RADIUS) &&
2502 VerifyField<float>(verifier, VT_BIAS) &&
2503 VerifyField<float>(verifier, VT_ALPHA) &&
2504 VerifyField<float>(verifier, VT_BETA) &&
2505 verifier.EndTable();
2506 }

2508 void UnPackTo(LocalResponseNormalizationOptionsT *_o, const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *_resolver = nullptr) const;
2509 static flatbuffers::Offset<LocalResponseNormalizationOptions> Pack(flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb, const LocalResponseNormalizationOptionsT* _o, const flatbuffers::rehasher_function_t *_rehasher = nullptr);

2938 VT_NGRAM_SIZE = 4,
2939 VT_MAX_SKIP_SIZE = 6,
2940 VT_INCLUDE_ALL_NGRAMS = 8
2941 };
2942 int32_t ngram_size() const {
2943 return GetField<int32_t>(VT_NGRAM_SIZE, 0);
2944 }
2945 int32_t max_skip_size() const {
2946 return GetField<int32_t>(VT_MAX_SKIP_SIZE, 0);
2947 }
2948 bool include_all_ngrams() const {
2949 return GetField<uint8_t>(VT_INCLUDE_ALL_NGRAMS, 0) != 0;
2950 }
2951 bool Verify(flatbuffers::Verifier &verifier) const {
2952 return VerifyTableStart(verifier) &&
2953 VerifyField<int32_t>(verifier, VT_NGRAM_SIZE) &&
2954 VerifyField<int32_t>(verifier, VT_MAX_SKIP_SIZE) &&
2955 VerifyField<uint8_t>(verifier, VT_INCLUDE_ALL_NGRAMS) &&
2956 verifier.EndTable();
2957 }
2958 SkipGramOptionsT *UnPack(const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *_resolver = nullptr) const;
2959 void UnPackTo(SkipGramOptionsT *_o, const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *_resolver = nullptr) const;
2960 static flatbuffers::Offset<SkipGramOptions> Pack(flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb, const SkipGramOptionsT* _o, const flatbuffers::rehasher_function_t *_rehasher = nullptr);
2961};

3457 const flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t> *squeeze_dims() const {
3458 return GetPointer<const flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t> *>(VT_SQUEEZE_DIMS);
3459 }
3460 bool Verify(flatbuffers::Verifier &verifier) const {
3461 return VerifyTableStart(verifier) &&
3462 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_SQUEEZE_DIMS) &&
3463 verifier.Verify(squeeze_dims()) &&
3464 verifier.EndTable();
3465 }
3466 SqueezeOptionsT *UnPack(const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *_resolver = nullptr) const;
3467 void UnPackTo(SqueezeOptionsT *_o, const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *_resolver = nullptr) const;
3468 static flatbuffers::Offset<SqueezeOptions> Pack(flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb, const SqueezeOptionsT* _o, const flatbuffers::rehasher_function_t *_rehasher = nullptr);
3469};

3925struct OperatorT : public flatbuffers::NativeTable {
3926 typedef Operator TableType;
3927 uint32_t opcode_index;
3928 std::vector<int32_t> inputs;
3929 std::vector<int32_t> outputs;
3930 BuiltinOptionsUnion builtin_options;
3931 std::vector<uint8_t> custom_options;
3932 CustomOptionsFormat custom_options_format;
3933 OperatorT()
3934 : opcode_index(0),
3935 custom_options_format(CustomOptionsFormat_FLEXBUFFERS) {
3936 }
3937};
3938
3939struct Operator FLATBUFFERS_FINAL_CLASS : private flatbuffers::Table {
3940 typedef OperatorT NativeTableType;
3941 enum {
3942 VT_OPCODE_INDEX = 4,
3943 VT_INPUTS = 6,
3944 VT_OUTPUTS = 8,
3945 VT_BUILTIN_OPTIONS_TYPE = 10,
3946 VT_BUILTIN_OPTIONS = 12,
3947 VT_CUSTOM_OPTIONS = 14,
3948 VT_CUSTOM_OPTIONS_FORMAT = 16
3949 };
3950 uint32_t opcode_index() const {
3951 return GetField<uint32_t>(VT_OPCODE_INDEX, 0);
3952 }
3953 const flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t> *inputs() const {
3954 return GetPointer<const flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t> *>(VT_INPUTS);
3955 }
3956 const flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t> *outputs() const {
3957 return GetPointer<const flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t> *>(VT_OUTPUTS);
3958 }
3959 BuiltinOptions builtin_options_type() const {
3960 return static_cast<BuiltinOptions>(GetField<uint8_t>(VT_BUILTIN_OPTIONS_TYPE, 0));
3961 }
3962 const void *builtin_options() const {
3963 return GetPointer<const void *>(VT_BUILTIN_OPTIONS);
3964 }
3965 template<typename T> const T *builtin_options_as() const;
3966 const Conv2DOptions *builtin_options_as_Conv2DOptions() const {
3967 return builtin_options_type() == BuiltinOptions_Conv2DOptions ? static_cast<const Conv2DOptions *>(builtin_options()) : nullptr;
3968 }
3969 const DepthwiseConv2DOptions *builtin_options_as_DepthwiseConv2DOptions() const {
3970 return builtin_options_type() == BuiltinOptions_DepthwiseConv2DOptions ? static_cast<const DepthwiseConv2DOptions *>(builtin_options()) : nullptr;
3971 }
3972 const ConcatEmbeddingsOptions *builtin_options_as_ConcatEmbeddingsOptions() const {
3973 return builtin_options_type() == BuiltinOptions_ConcatEmbeddingsOptions ? static_cast<const ConcatEmbeddingsOptions *>(builtin_options()) : nullptr;
3974 }
3975 const LSHProjectionOptions *builtin_options_as_LSHProjectionOptions() const {
3976 return builtin_options_type() == BuiltinOptions_LSHProjectionOptions ? static_cast<const LSHProjectionOptions *>(builtin_options()) : nullptr;
3977 }

4078 return builtin_options_type() == BuiltinOptions_DequantizeOptions ? static_cast<const DequantizeOptions *>(builtin_options()) : nullptr;
4079 }
4080 const MaximumOptions *builtin_options_as_MaximumOptions() const {
4081 return builtin_options_type() == BuiltinOptions_MaximumOptions ? static_cast<const MaximumOptions *>(builtin_options()) : nullptr;
4082 }
4083 const flatbuffers::Vector<uint8_t> *custom_options() const {
4084 return GetPointer<const flatbuffers::Vector<uint8_t> *>(VT_CUSTOM_OPTIONS);
4085 }
4086 CustomOptionsFormat custom_options_format() const {
4087 return static_cast<CustomOptionsFormat>(GetField<int8_t>(VT_CUSTOM_OPTIONS_FORMAT, 0));
4088 }
4089 bool Verify(flatbuffers::Verifier &verifier) const {
4090 return VerifyTableStart(verifier) &&
4091 VerifyField<uint32_t>(verifier, VT_OPCODE_INDEX) &&
4092 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_INPUTS) &&
4093 verifier.Verify(inputs()) &&
4094 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_OUTPUTS) &&
4095 verifier.Verify(outputs()) &&
4096 VerifyField<uint8_t>(verifier, VT_BUILTIN_OPTIONS_TYPE) &&
4097 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_BUILTIN_OPTIONS) &&
4098 VerifyBuiltinOptions(verifier, builtin_options(), builtin_options_type()) &&
4099 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_CUSTOM_OPTIONS) &&
4100 verifier.Verify(custom_options()) &&
4101 VerifyField<int8_t>(verifier, VT_CUSTOM_OPTIONS_FORMAT) &&
4102 verifier.EndTable();
4103 }
4104 OperatorT *UnPack(const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *_resolver = nullptr) const;
4105 void UnPackTo(OperatorT *_o, const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *_resolver = nullptr) const;
4106 static flatbuffers::Offset<Operator> Pack(flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb, const OperatorT* _o, const flatbuffers::rehasher_function_t *_rehasher = nullptr);
4107};

4265struct OperatorBuilder {
4266 flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &fbb_;
4267 flatbuffers::uoffset_t start_;
4268 void add_opcode_index(uint32_t opcode_index) {
4269 fbb_.AddElement<uint32_t>(Operator::VT_OPCODE_INDEX, opcode_index, 0);
4270 }
4271 void add_inputs(flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t>> inputs) {
4272 fbb_.AddOffset(Operator::VT_INPUTS, inputs);
4273 }
4274 void add_outputs(flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t>> outputs) {
4275 fbb_.AddOffset(Operator::VT_OUTPUTS, outputs);
4276 }
4277 void add_builtin_options_type(BuiltinOptions builtin_options_type) {
4278 fbb_.AddElement<uint8_t>(Operator::VT_BUILTIN_OPTIONS_TYPE, static_cast<uint8_t>(builtin_options_type), 0);
4279 }
4280 void add_builtin_options(flatbuffers::Offset<void> builtin_options) {
4281 fbb_.AddOffset(Operator::VT_BUILTIN_OPTIONS, builtin_options);
4282 }
4283 void add_custom_options(flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<uint8_t>> custom_options) {
4284 fbb_.AddOffset(Operator::VT_CUSTOM_OPTIONS, custom_options);
4285 }
4286 void add_custom_options_format(CustomOptionsFormat custom_options_format) {
4287 fbb_.AddElement<int8_t>(Operator::VT_CUSTOM_OPTIONS_FORMAT, static_cast<int8_t>(custom_options_format), 0);
4288 }
4289 explicit OperatorBuilder(flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb)
4290 : fbb_(_fbb) {
4291 start_ = fbb_.StartTable();
4292 }
4293 OperatorBuilder &operator=(const OperatorBuilder &);
4294 flatbuffers::Offset<Operator> Finish() {
4295 const auto end = fbb_.EndTable(start_);
4296 auto o = flatbuffers::Offset<Operator>(end);
4297 return o;
4298 }
4299};
4300
4301inline flatbuffers::Offset<Operator> CreateOperator(
4302 flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb,
4303 uint32_t opcode_index = 0,
4304 flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t>> inputs = 0,
4305 flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t>> outputs = 0,
4306 BuiltinOptions builtin_options_type = BuiltinOptions_NONE,
4307 flatbuffers::Offset<void> builtin_options = 0,
4308 flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<uint8_t>> custom_options = 0,
4309 CustomOptionsFormat custom_options_format = CustomOptionsFormat_FLEXBUFFERS) {
4310 OperatorBuilder builder_(_fbb);
4311 builder_.add_custom_options(custom_options);
4312 builder_.add_builtin_options(builtin_options);
4313 builder_.add_outputs(outputs);
4314 builder_.add_inputs(inputs);
4315 builder_.add_opcode_index(opcode_index);
4316 builder_.add_custom_options_format(custom_options_format);
4317 builder_.add_builtin_options_type(builtin_options_type);
4318 return builder_.Finish();
4319}

4321inline flatbuffers::Offset<Operator> CreateOperatorDirect(
4322 flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb,
4323 uint32_t opcode_index = 0,
4324 const std::vector<int32_t> *inputs = nullptr,
4325 const std::vector<int32_t> *outputs = nullptr,
4326 BuiltinOptions builtin_options_type = BuiltinOptions_NONE,
4327 flatbuffers::Offset<void> builtin_options = 0,
4328 const std::vector<uint8_t> *custom_options = nullptr,
4329 CustomOptionsFormat custom_options_format = CustomOptionsFormat_FLEXBUFFERS) {
4330 return tflite::CreateOperator(
4331 _fbb,
4332 opcode_index,
4333 inputs ? _fbb.CreateVector<int32_t>(*inputs) : 0,
4334 outputs ? _fbb.CreateVector<int32_t>(*outputs) : 0,
4335 builtin_options_type,
4336 builtin_options,
4337 custom_options ? _fbb.CreateVector<uint8_t>(*custom_options) : 0,
4338 custom_options_format);
4339}

4343struct SubGraphT : public flatbuffers::NativeTable {
4344 typedef SubGraph TableType;
4345 std::vector<std::unique_ptr<TensorT>> tensors;
4346 std::vector<int32_t> inputs;
4347 std::vector<int32_t> outputs;
4348 std::vector<std::unique_ptr<OperatorT>> operators;
4349 std::string name;
4350 SubGraphT() {
4351 }
4352};
4353
4354struct SubGraph FLATBUFFERS_FINAL_CLASS : private flatbuffers::Table {
4355 typedef SubGraphT NativeTableType;
4356 enum {
4357 VT_TENSORS = 4,
4358 VT_INPUTS = 6,
4359 VT_OUTPUTS = 8,
4360 VT_OPERATORS = 10,
4361 VT_NAME = 12
4362 };
4363 const flatbuffers::Vector<flatbuffers::Offset<Tensor>> *tensors() const {
4364 return GetPointer<const flatbuffers::Vector<flatbuffers::Offset<Tensor>> *>(VT_TENSORS);
4365 }
4366 const flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t> *inputs() const {
4367 return GetPointer<const flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t> *>(VT_INPUTS);
4368 }
4369 const flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t> *outputs() const {
4370 return GetPointer<const flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t> *>(VT_OUTPUTS);
4371 }
4372 const flatbuffers::Vector<flatbuffers::Offset<Operator>> *operators() const {
4373 return GetPointer<const flatbuffers::Vector<flatbuffers::Offset<Operator>> *>(VT_OPERATORS);
4374 }
4375 const flatbuffers::String *name() const {
4376 return GetPointer<const flatbuffers::String *>(VT_NAME);
4377 }
4378 bool Verify(flatbuffers::Verifier &verifier) const {
4379 return VerifyTableStart(verifier) &&
4380 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_TENSORS) &&
4381 verifier.Verify(tensors()) &&
4382 verifier.VerifyVectorOfTables(tensors()) &&
4383 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_INPUTS) &&
4384 verifier.Verify(inputs()) &&
4385 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_OUTPUTS) &&
4386 verifier.Verify(outputs()) &&
4387 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_OPERATORS) &&
4388 verifier.Verify(operators()) &&
4389 verifier.VerifyVectorOfTables(operators()) &&
4390 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_NAME) &&
4391 verifier.Verify(name()) &&
4392 verifier.EndTable();
4393 }
4394 SubGraphT *UnPack(const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *_resolver = nullptr) const;
4395 void UnPackTo(SubGraphT *_o, const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *_resolver = nullptr) const;
4396 static flatbuffers::Offset<SubGraph> Pack(flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb, const SubGraphT* _o, const flatbuffers::rehasher_function_t *_rehasher = nullptr);
4397};
4398
4399struct SubGraphBuilder {
4400 flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &fbb_;
4401 flatbuffers::uoffset_t start_;
4402 void add_tensors(flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<flatbuffers::Offset<Tensor>>> tensors) {
4403 fbb_.AddOffset(SubGraph::VT_TENSORS, tensors);
4404 }
4405 void add_inputs(flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t>> inputs) {
4406 fbb_.AddOffset(SubGraph::VT_INPUTS, inputs);
4407 }
4408 void add_outputs(flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t>> outputs) {
4409 fbb_.AddOffset(SubGraph::VT_OUTPUTS, outputs);
4410 }
4411 void add_operators(flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<flatbuffers::Offset<Operator>>> operators) {
4412 fbb_.AddOffset(SubGraph::VT_OPERATORS, operators);
4413 }
4414 void add_name(flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::String> name) {
4415 fbb_.AddOffset(SubGraph::VT_NAME, name);
4416 }
4417 explicit SubGraphBuilder(flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb)
4418 : fbb_(_fbb) {
4419 start_ = fbb_.StartTable();
4420 }
4421 SubGraphBuilder &operator=(const SubGraphBuilder &);
4422 flatbuffers::Offset<SubGraph> Finish() {
4423 const auto end = fbb_.EndTable(start_);
4424 auto o = flatbuffers::Offset<SubGraph>(end);
4425 return o;
4426 }
4427};
4428
4429inline flatbuffers::Offset<SubGraph> CreateSubGraph(
4430 flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb,
4431 flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<flatbuffers::Offset<Tensor>>> tensors = 0,
4432 flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t>> inputs = 0,
4433 flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<int32_t>> outputs = 0,
4434 flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<flatbuffers::Offset<Operator>>> operators = 0,
4435 flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::String> name = 0) {
4436 SubGraphBuilder builder_(_fbb);
4437 builder_.add_name(name);
4438 builder_.add_operators(operators);
4439 builder_.add_outputs(outputs);
4440 builder_.add_inputs(inputs);
4441 builder_.add_tensors(tensors);
4442 return builder_.Finish();
4443}
4444
4445inline flatbuffers::Offset<SubGraph> CreateSubGraphDirect(
4446 flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb,
4447 const std::vector<flatbuffers::Offset<Tensor>> *tensors = nullptr,
4448 const std::vector<int32_t> *inputs = nullptr,
4449 const std::vector<int32_t> *outputs = nullptr,
4450 const std::vector<flatbuffers::Offset<Operator>> *operators = nullptr,
4451 const char *name = nullptr) {
4452 return tflite::CreateSubGraph(
4453 _fbb,
4454 tensors ? _fbb.CreateVector<flatbuffers::Offset<Tensor>>(*tensors) : 0,
4455 inputs ? _fbb.CreateVector<int32_t>(*inputs) : 0,
4456 outputs ? _fbb.CreateVector<int32_t>(*outputs) : 0,
4457 operators ? _fbb.CreateVector<flatbuffers::Offset<Operator>>(*operators) : 0,
4458 name ? _fbb.CreateString(name) : 0);
4459}
4460
4461flatbuffers::Offset<SubGraph> CreateSubGraph(flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb, const SubGraphT *_o, const flatbuffers::rehasher_function_t *_rehasher = nullptr);
4462
4463struct BufferT : public flatbuffers::NativeTable {
4464 typedef Buffer TableType;
4465 std::vector<uint8_t> data;
4466 BufferT() {
4467 }
4468};
4469
4470struct Buffer FLATBUFFERS_FINAL_CLASS : private flatbuffers::Table {
4471 typedef BufferT NativeTableType;
4472 enum {
4473 VT_DATA = 4
4474 };
4475 const flatbuffers::Vector<uint8_t> *data() const {
4476 return GetPointer<const flatbuffers::Vector<uint8_t> *>(VT_DATA);
4477 }
4478 bool Verify(flatbuffers::Verifier &verifier) const {
4479 return VerifyTableStart(verifier) &&
4480 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_DATA) &&
4481 verifier.Verify(data()) &&
4482 verifier.EndTable();
4483 }
4484 BufferT *UnPack(const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *_resolver = nullptr) const;
4485 void UnPackTo(BufferT *_o, const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *_resolver = nullptr) const;
4486 static flatbuffers::Offset<Buffer> Pack(flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb, const BufferT* _o, const flatbuffers::rehasher_function_t *_rehasher = nullptr);
4487};
4488
4489struct BufferBuilder {
4490 flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &fbb_;
4491 flatbuffers::uoffset_t start_;
4492 void add_data(flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<uint8_t>> data) {
4493 fbb_.AddOffset(Buffer::VT_DATA, data);
4494 }
4495 explicit BufferBuilder(flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb)
4496 : fbb_(_fbb) {
4497 start_ = fbb_.StartTable();
4498 }
4499 BufferBuilder &operator=(const BufferBuilder &);
4500 flatbuffers::Offset<Buffer> Finish() {
4501 const auto end = fbb_.EndTable(start_);
4502 auto o = flatbuffers::Offset<Buffer>(end);
4503 return o;
4504 }
4505};
4506
4507inline flatbuffers::Offset<Buffer> CreateBuffer(
4508 flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb,
4509 flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<uint8_t>> data = 0) {
4510 BufferBuilder builder_(_fbb);
4511 builder_.add_data(data);
4512 return builder_.Finish();
4513}

4515inline flatbuffers::Offset<Buffer> CreateBufferDirect(
4516 flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb,
4517 const std::vector<uint8_t> *data = nullptr) {
4518 return tflite::CreateBuffer(
4519 _fbb,
4520 data ? _fbb.CreateVector<uint8_t>(*data) : 0);

4525struct ModelT : public flatbuffers::NativeTable {
4526 typedef Model TableType;
4527 uint32_t version;
4528 std::vector<std::unique_ptr<OperatorCodeT>> operator_codes;
4529 std::vector<std::unique_ptr<SubGraphT>> subgraphs;
4530 std::string description;
4531 std::vector<std::unique_ptr<BufferT>> buffers;
4532 ModelT()
4533 : version(0) {
4534 }
4535};
4536
4537struct Model FLATBUFFERS_FINAL_CLASS : private flatbuffers::Table {
4538 typedef ModelT NativeTableType;
4539 enum {
4540 VT_VERSION = 4,
4541 VT_OPERATOR_CODES = 6,
4542 VT_SUBGRAPHS = 8,
4543 VT_DESCRIPTION = 10,
4544 VT_BUFFERS = 12
4545 };
4546 uint32_t version() const {
4547 return GetField<uint32_t>(VT_VERSION, 0);
4548 }
4549 const flatbuffers::Vector<flatbuffers::Offset<OperatorCode>> *operator_codes() const {
4550 return GetPointer<const flatbuffers::Vector<flatbuffers::Offset<OperatorCode>> *>(VT_OPERATOR_CODES);
4551 }
4552 const flatbuffers::Vector<flatbuffers::Offset<SubGraph>> *subgraphs() const {
4553 return GetPointer<const flatbuffers::Vector<flatbuffers::Offset<SubGraph>> *>(VT_SUBGRAPHS);
4554 }
4555 const flatbuffers::String *description() const {
4556 return GetPointer<const flatbuffers::String *>(VT_DESCRIPTION);
4557 }
4558 const flatbuffers::Vector<flatbuffers::Offset<Buffer>> *buffers() const {
4559 return GetPointer<const flatbuffers::Vector<flatbuffers::Offset<Buffer>> *>(VT_BUFFERS);
4560 }
4561 bool Verify(flatbuffers::Verifier &verifier) const {
4562 return VerifyTableStart(verifier) &&
4563 VerifyField<uint32_t>(verifier, VT_VERSION) &&
4564 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_OPERATOR_CODES) &&
4565 verifier.Verify(operator_codes()) &&
4566 verifier.VerifyVectorOfTables(operator_codes()) &&
4567 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_SUBGRAPHS) &&
4568 verifier.Verify(subgraphs()) &&
4569 verifier.VerifyVectorOfTables(subgraphs()) &&
4570 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_DESCRIPTION) &&
4571 verifier.Verify(description()) &&
4572 VerifyOffset(verifier, VT_BUFFERS) &&
4573 verifier.Verify(buffers()) &&
4574 verifier.VerifyVectorOfTables(buffers()) &&
4575 verifier.EndTable();
4576 }
4577 ModelT *UnPack(const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *_resolver = nullptr) const;
4578 void UnPackTo(ModelT *_o, const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *_resolver = nullptr) const;
4579 static flatbuffers::Offset<Model> Pack(flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb, const ModelT* _o, const flatbuffers::rehasher_function_t *_rehasher = nullptr);
4580};
4581
4582struct ModelBuilder {
4583 flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &fbb_;
4584 flatbuffers::uoffset_t start_;
4585 void add_version(uint32_t version) {
4586 fbb_.AddElement<uint32_t>(Model::VT_VERSION, version, 0);
4587 }
4588 void add_operator_codes(flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<flatbuffers::Offset<OperatorCode>>> operator_codes) {
4589 fbb_.AddOffset(Model::VT_OPERATOR_CODES, operator_codes);
4590 }
4591 void add_subgraphs(flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<flatbuffers::Offset<SubGraph>>> subgraphs) {
4592 fbb_.AddOffset(Model::VT_SUBGRAPHS, subgraphs);
4593 }
4594 void add_description(flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::String> description) {
4595 fbb_.AddOffset(Model::VT_DESCRIPTION, description);
4596 }
4597 void add_buffers(flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<flatbuffers::Offset<Buffer>>> buffers) {
4598 fbb_.AddOffset(Model::VT_BUFFERS, buffers);
4599 }
4600 explicit ModelBuilder(flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb)
4601 : fbb_(_fbb) {
4602 start_ = fbb_.StartTable();
4603 }
4604 ModelBuilder &operator=(const ModelBuilder &);
4605 flatbuffers::Offset<Model> Finish() {
4606 const auto end = fbb_.EndTable(start_);
4607 auto o = flatbuffers::Offset<Model>(end);
4608 return o;
4609 }
4610};

4612inline flatbuffers::Offset<Model> CreateModel(
4613 flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb,
4614 uint32_t version = 0,
4615 flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<flatbuffers::Offset<OperatorCode>>> operator_codes = 0,
4616 flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<flatbuffers::Offset<SubGraph>>> subgraphs = 0,
4617 flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::String> description = 0,
4618 flatbuffers::Offset<flatbuffers::Vector<flatbuffers::Offset<Buffer>>> buffers = 0) {
4619 ModelBuilder builder_(_fbb);
4620 builder_.add_buffers(buffers);
4621 builder_.add_description(description);
4622 builder_.add_subgraphs(subgraphs);
4623 builder_.add_operator_codes(operator_codes);
4624 builder_.add_version(version);
4625 return builder_.Finish();
4626}

5856
5857inline void Operator::UnPackTo(OperatorT *_o, const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *_resolver) const {
5858 (void)_o;
5859 (void)_resolver;
5860 { auto _e = opcode_index(); _o->opcode_index = _e; };
5861 { auto _e = inputs(); if (_e) { _o->inputs.resize(_e->size()); for (flatbuffers::uoffset_t _i = 0; _i < _e->size(); _i++) { _o->inputs[_i] = _e->Get(_i); } } };
5862 { auto _e = outputs(); if (_e) { _o->outputs.resize(_e->size()); for (flatbuffers::uoffset_t _i = 0; _i < _e->size(); _i++) { _o->outputs[_i] = _e->Get(_i); } } };
5863 { auto _e = builtin_options_type(); _o->builtin_options.type = _e; };
5864 { auto _e = builtin_options(); if (_e) _o->builtin_options.value = BuiltinOptionsUnion::UnPack(_e, builtin_options_type(), _resolver); };
5865 { auto _e = custom_options(); if (_e) { _o->custom_options.resize(_e->size()); for (flatbuffers::uoffset_t _i = 0; _i < _e->size(); _i++) { _o->custom_options[_i] = _e->Get(_i); } } };
5866 { auto _e = custom_options_format(); _o->custom_options_format = _e; };
5867}

5871}
5872
5873inline flatbuffers::Offset<Operator> CreateOperator(flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb, const OperatorT *_o, const flatbuffers::rehasher_function_t *_rehasher) {
5874 (void)_rehasher;
5875 (void)_o;
5876 struct _VectorArgs { flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder *__fbb; const OperatorT* __o; const flatbuffers::rehasher_function_t *__rehasher; } _va = { &_fbb, _o, _rehasher}; (void)_va;
5877 auto _opcode_index = _o->opcode_index;
5878 auto _inputs = _o->inputs.size() ? _fbb.CreateVector(_o->inputs) : 0;
5879 auto _outputs = _o->outputs.size() ? _fbb.CreateVector(_o->outputs) : 0;
5880 auto _builtin_options_type = _o->builtin_options.type;
5881 auto _builtin_options = _o->builtin_options.Pack(_fbb);
5882 auto _custom_options = _o->custom_options.size() ? _fbb.CreateVector(_o->custom_options) : 0;
5883 auto _custom_options_format = _o->custom_options_format;
5884 return tflite::CreateOperator(
5885 _fbb,
5886 _opcode_index,
5887 _inputs,
5888 _outputs,
5889 _builtin_options_type,
5890 _builtin_options,
5891 _custom_options,
5892 _custom_options_format);
5893}

5901inline void SubGraph::UnPackTo(SubGraphT *_o, const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *_resolver) const {

5908 { auto _e = name(); if (_e) _o->name = _e->str(); };

5915inline flatbuffers::Offset<SubGraph> CreateSubGraph(flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb, const SubGraphT *_o, const flatbuffers::rehasher_function_t *_rehasher) {
5916 (void)_rehasher;
5917 (void)_o;
5918 struct _VectorArgs { flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder *__fbb; const SubGraphT* __o; const flatbuffers::rehasher_function_t *__rehasher; } _va = { &_fbb, _o, _rehasher}; (void)_va;
5919 auto _tensors = _o->tensors.size() ? _fbb.CreateVector<flatbuffers::Offset<Tensor>> (_o->tensors.size(), [](size_t i, _VectorArgs *__va) { return CreateTensor(*__va->__fbb, __va->__o->tensors[i].get(), __va->__rehasher); }, &_va ) : 0;
5920 auto _inputs = _o->inputs.size() ? _fbb.CreateVector(_o->inputs) : 0;
5921 auto _outputs = _o->outputs.size() ? _fbb.CreateVector(_o->outputs) : 0;
5922 auto _operators = _o->operators.size() ? _fbb.CreateVector<flatbuffers::Offset<Operator>> (_o->operators.size(), [](size_t i, _VectorArgs *__va) { return CreateOperator(*__va->__fbb, __va->__o->operators[i].get(), __va->__rehasher); }, &_va ) : 0;
5923 auto _name = _o->name.empty() ? 0 : _fbb.CreateString(_o->name);
5924 return tflite::CreateSubGraph(
5925 _fbb,
5926 _tensors,
5927 _inputs,
5928 _outputs,
5929 _operators,
5930 _name);
5931}

5979inline flatbuffers::Offset<Model> CreateModel(flatbuffers::FlatBufferBuilder &_fbb, const ModelT *_o, const flatbuffers::rehasher_function_t *_rehasher) {
5980 (void)_rehasher;

5983 auto _version = _o->version;

5985 auto _subgraphs = _o->subgraphs.size() ? _fbb.CreateVector<flatbuffers::Offset<SubGraph>> (_o->subgraphs.size(), [](size_t i, _VectorArgs *__va) { return CreateSubGraph(*__va->__fbb, __va->__o->subgraphs[i].get(), __va->__rehasher); }, &_va ) : 0;
5986 auto _description = _o->description.empty() ? 0 : _fbb.CreateString(_o->description);
5987 auto _buffers = _o->buffers.size() ? _fbb.CreateVector<flatbuffers::Offset<Buffer>> (_o->buffers.size(), [](size_t i, _VectorArgs *__va) { return CreateBuffer(*__va->__fbb, __va->__o->buffers[i].get(), __va->__rehasher); }, &_va ) : 0;
5988 return tflite::CreateModel(
5989 _fbb,
5990 _version,
5991 _operator_codes,
5992 _subgraphs,
5993 _description,
5994 _buffers);

5997inline bool VerifyBuiltinOptions(flatbuffers::Verifier &verifier, const void *obj, BuiltinOptions type) {
5998 switch (type) {
5999 case BuiltinOptions_NONE: {
6000 return true;
6001 }
6002 case BuiltinOptions_Conv2DOptions: {

6004 return verifier.VerifyTable(ptr);
6005 }
6006 case BuiltinOptions_DepthwiseConv2DOptions: {
6007 auto ptr = reinterpret_cast<const DepthwiseConv2DOptions *>(obj);
6008 return verifier.VerifyTable(ptr);

6012 return verifier.VerifyTable(ptr);

6020 return verifier.VerifyTable(ptr);
6021 }

6036 return verifier.VerifyTable(ptr);

6161
6162inline bool VerifyBuiltinOptionsVector(flatbuffers::Verifier &verifier, const flatbuffers::Vector<flatbuffers::Offset<void>> *values, const flatbuffers::Vector<uint8_t> *types) {
6163 if (!values || !types) return !values && !types;
6164 if (values->size() != types->size()) return false;
6165 for (flatbuffers::uoffset_t i = 0; i < values->size(); ++i) {
6166 if (!VerifyBuiltinOptions(
6167 verifier, values->Get(i), types->GetEnum<BuiltinOptions>(i))) {
6168 return false;
6169 }
6170 }
6171 return true;
6172}
6173
6174inline void *BuiltinOptionsUnion::UnPack(const void *obj, BuiltinOptions type, const flatbuffers::resolver_function_t *resolver) {
6175 switch (type) {
6176 case BuiltinOptions_Conv2DOptions: {
6177 auto ptr = reinterpret_cast<const Conv2DOptions *>(obj);
6178 return ptr->UnPack(resolver);
6179 }
6180 case BuiltinOptions_DepthwiseConv2DOptions: {
6181 auto ptr = reinterpret_cast<const DepthwiseConv2DOptions *>(obj);
6182 return ptr->UnPack(resolver);
6183 }
6184 case BuiltinOptions_ConcatEmbeddingsOptions: {
6185 auto ptr = reinterpret_cast<const ConcatEmbeddingsOptions *>(obj);
6186 return ptr->UnPack(resolver);
6187 }
6188 case BuiltinOptions_LSHProjectionOptions: {
6189 auto ptr = reinterpret_cast<const LSHProjectionOptions *>(obj);
6190 return ptr->UnPack(resolver);
6191 }
6192 case BuiltinOptions_Pool2DOptions: {
6193 auto ptr = reinterpret_cast<const Pool2DOptions *>(obj);
6194 return ptr->UnPack(resolver);
6195 }
6196 case BuiltinOptions_SVDFOptions: {
6197 auto ptr = reinterpret_cast<const SVDFOptions *>(obj);
6198 return ptr->UnPack(resolver);
6199 }
6200 case BuiltinOptions_RNNOptions: {
6201 auto ptr = reinterpret_cast<const RNNOptions *>(obj);
6202 return ptr->UnPack(resolver);
6203 }
6204 case BuiltinOptions_FullyConnectedOptions: {
6205 auto ptr = reinterpret_cast<const FullyConnectedOptions *>(obj);
6206 return ptr->UnPack(resolver);
6207 }
6208 case BuiltinOptions_SoftmaxOptions: {
6209 auto ptr = reinterpret_cast<const SoftmaxOptions *>(obj);
6210 return ptr->UnPack(resolver);
6211 }
6212 case BuiltinOptions_ConcatenationOptions: {
6213 auto ptr = reinterpret_cast<const ConcatenationOptions *>(obj);
6214 return ptr->UnPack(resolver);
6215 }
6216 case BuiltinOptions_AddOptions: {
6217 auto ptr = reinterpret_cast<const AddOptions *>(obj);
6218 return ptr->UnPack(resolver);
6219 }
6220 case BuiltinOptions_L2NormOptions: {
6221 auto ptr = reinterpret_cast<const L2NormOptions *>(obj);
6222 return ptr->UnPack(resolver);
6223 }

6843 case BuiltinOptions_CastOptions: {
6844 auto ptr = reinterpret_cast<CastOptionsT *>(value);
6845 delete ptr;
6846 break;
6847 }
6848 case BuiltinOptions_DequantizeOptions: {
6849 auto ptr = reinterpret_cast<DequantizeOptionsT *>(value);
6850 delete ptr;
6851 break;
6852 }
6853 case BuiltinOptions_MaximumOptions: {
6854 auto ptr = reinterpret_cast<MaximumOptionsT *>(value);
6855 delete ptr;
6856 break;
6857 }
6858 default: break;
6859 }
6860 value = nullptr;
6861 type = BuiltinOptions_NONE;
6862}

6865 return flatbuffers::GetRoot<tflite::Model>(buf);
